DMAR NAG GSAN NAS LAS SBYOR GYI MTHU KHANG LAG MTHUS GLAGS

ZLA GRANG DUS YIN RUNG BRAG LAS SGRUB CHU GLO BUR DU BABS BA
PHYAG PHYI BA RNAMS KYIS LCE THOG TU MYONG ZHING YID CHES KYI
GNAS SU GYUR, YUM BGRES MOS GSOL BA BTAB PA BRTEN GZHIS KAR ZLA
BA LNGA TZAM GYI

DBYANGS KYIS THIG RTZA BGYIS PA'I THUGS RTEN GSER DNGUL LAS GRUB
PA'I BYANG CHUB

PA, RING BSREL RNAM PA BZHI DANG GNOD SBYIN 'KHOR LO KHYAD PAR
DRI MED NAS GSUNGS PA'I SROG SHING 'DZUGS PA'I CHOG THAMS CAD
MKHYEN PA MKHYEN BRTZE'I

DBANG PHYUG GI PHYAG BZHES LTAR DBON MKHYEN RAB BLO LDAN, MCHOD
DPON 'JAM DBYANGS RGYAL MTSAR, DGE SLONG SANGS RGYAS DBANG PHYUG
GSUM GYIS LAG BSTAR, BZHUGS GNAS GTZUG LAG KHANG ZHIG GSOS LA
BRTEN PA'I RGYA

DANG DPANGS BSTOD PAR BZHUGS SU GSOL SKU RTEN LA BLA CHAS CHA
'GRIG, GSUNG RTEN DANG GDUNG RTEN LA KHRI, THUN MONG DU SA RGYAN,
GNAM RGYAN, MCHOD RDZAS KYI RIM PA TSAR DU DNGAR BA ZLA BA BZHI'I
KHONGS SU LEGS PAR GRUB PA

RGYA MTSOS RDO RJE SLOB DPON MDZAD DE GNYUG MAR GNAS PA'I DGE

RAS BRIS KYI DKYIL 'KHOR LA BRTEN PA'I

PA'I NGO MCHAR MTHA'
